## 9:21. October MOTM rematch, with Hijo del Villano replacing Villano Jr. (injury) and changed to a lightning match.

## 13:13. 4th defense. Templario had Brillante as a second, Volador Jr. had Rugido. Rugido snuck in late in the match to German suplex Templario' Templario kicked out. The rudos set up the tecnicos for splashes through tables, but Vikingo came out and attacked Alberto to start the comeback.
